MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because both parties have agreed on a price of $39 per unit. The answer is Yes.

---- start bargaining ----
  seller: 我很抱歉，但我们不能接受每单元$30的价格。我们的起始价格是$50，您能否考虑提高您的报价？【violation】
  buyer: 你会考虑以每单元$30的价格进行出售吗？
---- start moderating ----
MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because both parties have agreed on the price of $40 and are looking forward to establishing a good cooperation relationship. The answer is Yes.

MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because both parties have agreed to a price of $37 per unit. The answer is Yes.
